RT News 11.09.2021 11:00:12
Increasing number of Australians are seeking to leave their country (Report)

The Australian Border Force (ABF) received almost 40,000 applications in August from individuals hoping to leave the country ‚Äì of which 14,900 of those were looking to be overseas for 3 months or more. (Epoch Times)

A large portion of the applications, 12,347, were rejected. Australia is one of the few countries in the world that require residents to apply for permission before leaving the country.

Australia has enjoyed some of the lowest infection and death rates from COVID-19 but it has seen state governments apply stringent health restrictions and domestic border closures at any sign of an outbreak ‚Äì sometimes over 1 case.

The president of a conservative think tank told the Daily Telegraph: ‚ÄúThere are literally tens of thousands of people out there on social media and elsewhere saying we‚Äôre done; we don‚Äôt need this anymore.‚Äù

Good news! SOMEONE IN ANOTHER GROUP got off a meeting with the Justice Centre for Constitutional Rights. They are moving forward with a class action suite against the government. They are looking for people to join who have been impacted by mandatory vaccine passports, they are looking specifically for parents with kids that are being excluded from sports or school, university students and business owners who do not want to enforce vaccine passports. They said this case could take 10 months (based in Toronto supreme court) but you only need to sign an affidavit, not participate in court. Most importantly you need to be OK with your name being public and associated to to this case. There is no cost to be part of this. If you are interested, you can submit this form with your information https://www.jccf.ca/contact-information/
i will cross post this to a few other groups I am part of.

COPY and PASTED .... BE AWARE.... I've seen tons of posts. Stand ur ground call ur PPC candidate if they are not on the list. Don't fill in their name that ISNT how you vote


My partner and I went to vote at the Elections Canada office at 920 Boul. Saint-Joseph, Gatineau QC today for advanced voting.

The Elections Supervisor proceeded to ID us, confirm our voter cards, then insisted we use a PENCIL, not a pen, to WRITE OUT (not choose) the name of our preferred candidate on a piece of paper. When I pushed back against the use of a pencil in lieu of pen, he conceded and muttered something about pen being acceptable only as of this election (not previous elections).

When presented with the list of Party Candidates, we noticed that our local #PPC candidate David Bruce Gottfred was nowhere to be found!

I asked the Elections supervisor why our Pontiac PPC candidate was missing from the list of candidate choices, and he replied; ‚Äúyour candidate appears to not have amassed enough support - a minimum of 100 nominations, to be included on the ballot.‚Äù

I was stunned to say the least.

After asking to speak to his superior, another woman walks in and they deliberate for a few minutes, while I proceed to message my PPC representative about what I was seeing.

After a short discussion outside of the office (and out of ear/view of my partner and I), they returned and affirmed that our PPC representative was indeed missing, and they proceeded to add Bruce‚Äôs name in messy handwriting at the bottom of the candidate list.

Again, the handling of this is shocking behaviour for a Federal Elections office.

We cast our vote IN PEN, put our written ballot in an Elections Canada envelope, deposited in the ballot box, and before departing, I reiterated our disappointment and repeatedly requested that all candidate lists be updated to reflect the proper information, including party representatives that have been ‚Äúomitted‚Äù.

Our democratic election process is being mishandled, undermined and corrupted.

Rob Boutilier Maxime Bernier Randy Hillier- take note. #PPC2021 #Election2021 #canadavotes

EDIT: I‚Äôve filed a formal complaint to the Office of Elections Canada.

Reg. 364/20: RULES FOR AREAS AT STEP 3 AND AT THE ROADMAP EXIT STEP which can be found at https://www.ontario.ca/laws/regulation/200364#BK9 speaks to masking for indoor recreational facilities. Section 2 General Compliance refers to masks and face coverings, while and Section 16 is more in-depth for indoor recreational facilities. I have copied section 2 that speaks to masking. I recommend you to reach out to the London Gymnastics Academy to inquire if they have implemented more stringent rules for their patrons and facility.
General compliance

2. (1) The person responsible for a business or organization that is open shall ensure that the business or organization operates in accordance with all applicable laws, including the Occupational Health and Safety Act and the regulations made under it.

(4) Where there is any requirement under this Order that a person wear a mask or face covering, the requirement does not apply to a person who,

(i) needs to temporarily remove their mask or face covering while in the indoor area,

(i) to receive services that require the removal of their mask or face covering,

(ii) to engage in an athletic or fitness activity,

(iii) to consume food or drink, or

(iv) as may be necessary for the purposes of health and safety

–ù–µ—Ç, –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥—É—Ç, –≤ —ç—Ç–æ–º —Ç–æ –∏ —Ñ–∏—à–∫–∞. –í–æ—Ç —á—Ç–æ —è —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏–ª–∞ –¥–ª—è —Å–µ–±—è (–∏ —Å–æ–±–∏—Ä–∞—é—Å—å –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —É–∂–µ –°–ï–ì–û–î–ù–Ø) –ø–æ –ø–æ–≤–æ–¥—É Trespass to Property Act, sec.#2
09:49
My vaccination information is private. I am allowed to be served in an equal manner as the rest of the patrons without discrimination. I am not willing to leave because it violates my human rights code of Ontario to not be served in the same manner as the rest of the patrons.
Trespass is not a criminal offense so police will not arrest trespassers unless they believe they are committing or intend to commit aggravated trespass; a further act beyond the actual trespass intended to ‚Äúdeter, disrupt or obstruct‚Äù the lawful business taking place.
We are not trespassing. It's not private but public property. I am showing you the law.
ÔÅ∂ #1 - the Immunization act of 1997: in Canada you cannot mandate vaccinations. It's a Federal law and it supersedes the trespass regulation even if it was applicable here and it is not. You have no right to ask me to be immunized in order to come here. Under the law I have the right to come here and use the service that they‚Äôve advertised for us to use.
ÔÅ∂ Trespass to Property Act, sec.#2 states that as long as you are in here taking part in the business as they advertise it‚Äôs not applicable. The Trespass act is not applicable to this circumstances. Section 2 of the Trespass Act reads as follows:
1) Every person who is not acting under a right or authority conferred by law and who,
(a) without the express permission of the occupier, the proof of which rests on the defendant,
(i) enters on premises when entry is prohibited under this Act, or
(ii) engages in an activity on premises when the activity is prohibited under this Act; or
(b) does not leave the premises immediately after he or she is directed to do so by the occupier of the premises or a person authorized by the occupier,
is guilty of an offence.
I trespass if the owner or administration #1 - asks me to leave and #2 ‚Äì only if I do NOT act under a right or authority conferred by law. Businesses operating under municipal or provincial license operate with the general invitation for the public to enter. Once I enter the premises and I exercise my lawful right to NOT disclose my vaccination status under the Federal and Provincial regulations I am acting under a right or authority conferred by law.
The fact that you ask me to leave is only one of the 2 requirements for me to be trespassing. I also have to be in the premises without a right conferred under the Law. So I have the right under the Law and authority by Ontario regulations to exercise my right NOT to disclose my vaccine status. I only meet one of the 2 criteria necessary to be trespassing. So, in this circumstances under section 2, I am NOT trespassing. In the same way a store owner or building administration cannot ask me to leave just because I am a woman or I am black or a South Asian or any other prohibited grounds under the Human Rights Code. They cannot simply ask me to leave because I refuse to disclose my vaccine status because this exemption is part of the Law and I am acting under the Law. The store owner cannot arbitrarily simply say get out or I will charge you with Trespass. In fact, the store owner or building administration in these circumstances is breaking the law as well as the police officer who is enforcing this illegal order from the store owner.
Often people confuse removal from the property for purported trespass when they are in fact removed from ugly or criminal behavior. If a person is breaking a law such as mischief or assault or uttering threats the police can remove them. But that has nothing to do with trespassing because this is a breach of the criminal law.
09:49
And this is NOT a private property in a sense of a farm or a residence. It is property on which there is a business that's governed by a license from the municipality or the Province. The license to conduct the business states whereby the members of the public have an open invitation to buy goods or use the services and is governed by the law which includes the human rights code. You cannot make up your own law when you are licensed by municipal or provincial licensing regulation. You cannot treat your business as if it is your private home and put up a trespass sign at will whenever you feel like it.

All businesses are governed by a license from the municipality or the Province. The license to conduct the business states whereby the members of the public have an open invitation to buy goods or use the services and is governed by the law which includes the human rights code. You cannot make up your own law when you are licensed by municipal or provincial licensing regulation.

AS
April Shower 27.09.2021 20:08:52
From fb group against mandatory jab. Verified by several other nurses.


This from a blog that I am on:

"So, I have mentioned on here multiple times that my wife's a nurse at a hospital. Last night she worked an extra shift in the Emergency Room (not her regular department).

She found out, how "they" are getting away with claiming there's a "pandemic of the unvaccinated."

While dealing with a patient who came in exhibiting symptoms of myocarditis, a FT Emergency Room nurse conveyed some very interesting information to my wife. Apparently, all patients are asked whether or not they received the #CV19 vax, no matter what issue it is that brought them into the ER.

If the patient received the vax less than 14 days prior, they are recorded as "Un-Vaxxed" The story the nurses are being given, is that this is done because the vax takes 14 days to start working. The FT ER nurse my wife talked to last night has a different theory: It has been her observation that most patients coming in with what appears to be vaccine injuries are coming in within 72 hours of receiving the jab. By recording these patients as "Un-Vaxxed" they can do a few things:

- one, they can claim those vax injuries are a result of Covid & not the shot.

- two, they can bury the vaccine injury.

- three, they get to claim there's a "pandemic of the unvaccinated." It also turns out that nurses are being required to sign nondisclosure agreements, promising not to publicly discuss any procedures dealing with #CV19.

My wife refused to sign this agreement, and she's awaiting possible retaliatory response from upper mgmt. We need nurses across the country to start talking about all of this openly, as I'm sure our little hospital is not the only place this is occurring."
